10
constraint
0
expression(wasNotGiven = true) or explanation.reasonNotGiven.empty()
humanIf immunization was administered (wasNotGiven=false) then explanation.reasonNotGiven SHALL be absent.
keyimm-2
severityerror
xpathnot(f:wasNotGiven/@value=false() and exists(f:explanation/f:reasonNotGiven))
1
expression(wasNotGiven = true).not() or (reaction.empty() and explanation.reason.empty())
humanIf immunization was not administered (wasNotGiven=true) then there SHALL be no reaction nor explanation.reason present
keyimm-1
severityerror
xpathnot(f:wasNotGiven/@value=true() and (count(f:reaction) > 0 or exists(f:explanation/f:reason)))
